            window.loadScript = function(src, done, id, type = 'text/javascript') {
              var tag = document.createElement('script');
              tag.async = false;
              tag.src = src;
              tag.id = id;
              tag.setAttribute('data-ot-ignore', '');
              tag.type = type;
              if (done) {
                  tag.onload = function() {
                    done()
                  }
              }
              if (done) {
                  tag.onerror=function(){
                    done()
                  }
              }
              document.head.appendChild(tag);
            }
